---
title: "HasSynchronizeWithReaders"
description: "Mix-in for keeping track of a set of the readers. Used for implementing the HasSynchronizeWithClosing logic: Each computation acquires one permit before it starts and released it when done. HasSynchronizeWithReaders.synchronizeWithReaders attempts to acquire all permits and logs progress if slow."
---

## HasSynchronizeWithReaders - stable

Upstream docs: [Open](<https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/lifecycle/HasSynchronizeWithReaders.html>)

**Signature**

```text
trait HasSynchronizeWithReaders extends HasSynchronizeWithClosing
```
